id="id8dd271a05fd42589cbe75a953e521d7_4"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Q2 Results and Forecast</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Our Q2 revenue increased by 16% year over year (17% on a foreign exchange (F&#47;X) neutral basis</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">). Year-over-year revenue growth was primarily a function of more members, higher subscription pricing and increased ad revenue. All regions experienced healthy year-over-year revenue growth, with each region posting double-digit F&#47;X neutral increases. UCAN revenue growth accelerated year over year to 15% vs. 9% in Q1&#8217;25 due to the full quarter impact of price changes.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Revenue was slightly above our guidance due primarily to favorable F&#47;X impact, net of hedging. Member growth was ahead of our forecast, although this occurred late in the quarter, limiting the impact on Q2 revenue. Operating income totaled $3.8B, up 45% year over year, and operating margin was 34% vs 27% in Q2&#8217;24. Both operating income and operating margin were slightly ahead of our forecast given the revenue upside in the quarter and timing of expense spending. Diluted EPS amounted to $7.19 vs. $4.88 last year (+47% year over year). </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As a reminder, the guidance we provide is our actual internal forecast at the time we report and we strive for accuracy. Our primary financial metrics are revenue for growth and operating margin for profitability. Our goal is to sustain healthy revenue growth, expand operating margin and deliver growing free cash flow. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">In Q3&#8217;25, we expect revenue growth of 17% (on both a reported and F&#47;X neutral basis) driven by growth in members, pricing and advertising revenue. We project operating margin of 31%, a two percentage point year-over-year improvement. Similar to past years, we expect our operating margin in the second half of 2025 will be lower than the first half due to higher content amortization and sales and marketing costs associated with our larger second half slate.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For 2025, we are increasing our revenue forecast to $44.8B-$45.2B from $43.5B-$44.5B, previously. This represents 15%-16% year-over-year growth, or 16%-17% growth on a F&#47;X neutral basis. The majority of the increase in our revenue forecast reflects the recent depreciation of the US dollar vs. most other currencies, with the balance attributable to continued business momentum driven by solid member growth and ad sales. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As a result, we are now targeting a 29.5% operating margin for 2025, based on F&#47;X rates at the beginning of the year, up from our prior 29% forecast. At current F&#47;X rates, this would equate to roughly a 30% operating margin for 2025 on a reported basis. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Content &#38; Engagement</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Our goal is to offer a wide variety of quality series, films and games that our members love. This in turn drives engagement on Netflix and when people watch more and love what they watch, they stick around longer (retention), recommend Netflix to others (acquisition) and place a higher value on our service. We monetize this engagement through both subscription and advertising revenue.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">__________________________________</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">2 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Excluding the year over year effect of foreign exchange rate movements and the impact of hedging gains&#47;losses realized as revenues. It&#8217;s the </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">highest-charting soundtrack</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">6 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">of 2025 on the Billboard 200 and just this week, </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">&#34;Golden&#34; hit #1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">7</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> on the Billboard Global Charts, becoming the biggest song in the world. The soundtrack is currently the #1 movie soundtrack on Spotify, is the first K-pop album to ever be #1 on the US Apple Music chart and on iTunes charts simultaneously, and there are seven tracks from the album on the </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Billboard Hot 100</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">8</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:12.53pt">Finally, our Q2 slate wrapped up on a high note with </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> S3* (122M views), which has already become our sixth biggest season of any series in our history, with just a few weeks of viewing so far. Korean content continues to be popular with our audience. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">At Netflix, our content strategy is Building on this momentum, in June we announced an investment of over </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">one billion Euros in Spain</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">13</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> between 2025-2028 to further expand our Spanish programming slate. As we saw with </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> from South Korea, every so often a show becomes a true global phenomenon&#8212;captivating audiences not just in its home country, but around the world. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> was created first and foremost for Korean viewers, but its authentic storytelling and universal themes resonated far beyond Korea&#8217;s borders.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As we grow globally, our most significant investment </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">remains in the US</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">14</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, which accounts for the majority of our content spend, workforce and production infrastructure. From 2020-2024, we estimate that we contributed $125 billion to the US economy. Our expansion in Albuquerque, NM&#8212;adding four new soundstages to a 108-acre site&#8212;and our plan to invest roughly $1B to develop a state-of-the-art production facility (including 12 new soundstages) in Fort Monmouth, NJ, underscore our ongoing commitment to production in the US. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We recently announced a </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">partnership</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">15</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> with leading local broadcaster TF1 in France which will allow us to offer TF1&#8217;s linear channels and on-demand content to our French members as part of their Netflix subscription without having to leave our service. The wide variety of additional content will include local titles and genres like soap operas, big weekly competition shows and major live sports programming such as the UEFA Nations League that is incremental to what we offer our members today. The partnership will go live in the summer of 2026 and we expect to learn about the value this expanded local programming can provide our members.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We continue to invest in immersive, narrative games based on our IP. For example, in Q2 in conjunction with </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Black Mirror</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> S7, we launched </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Thronglets</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, the game at the center of the episode &#8220;Plaything.&#8221; The mobile game immersed fans in the world of </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Black Mirror</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> like never before. And, alongside the series finale of </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter and its attachments include reference to the non-GAAP financial measures of F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin, free cash flow and net debt. Management believes that free cash flow is an important liquidity metric because it measures, during a given period, the amount of cash generated that is available to repay debt obligations, make strategic acquisitions and investments and for certain other activities like stock repurchases. Management believes that F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin allow investors to compare our projected results to our actual results absent year-over-year and intra-year currency fluctuations, respectively, and the impact of restructuring costs. Management believes net debt is a useful measure of the company's liquidity, capital structure, and leverage. However, these non-GAAP financial measures should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, net income, operating income (profit), operating margin, diluted earnings per share and net cash provided by (used in) operating activities, or other financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. Reconciliation to the GAAP equivalent of these non-GAAP measures are contained in tabular form on the attached unaudited financial statements and in the F&#47;X neutral operating margin disclosure above. We are not able to reconcile forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures because we are unable to predict without unreasonable effort the exact amount or timing of the reconciling items, including property and equipment and change in other assets, and the impact of changes in currency exchange rates. The variability of these items could have a significant impact on our future GAAP financial results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws, including statements regarding our expected results for the fiscal quarter ending September 30, 2025 and fiscal year ending December 31, 2025&#59; priorities for 2025&#59; adoption and growth of streaming entertainment&#59; growth strategy and outlook&#59; investments&#59; partnerships&#59; market opportunity&#59; competitive landscape and position&#59; entertainment offerings, including TV shows, movies, games, and live programming&#59; engagement&#59; production infrastructure&#59; slate strength&#59; pricing and plans strategy&#59; ad-supported tier and its prospects&#59; advertising, including sales and our ad-tech platform&#59; product strategy, including redesigned TV interface and recommendations&#59; impact of foreign exchange rates&#59; foreign currency exchange hedging program&#59; stock repurchases&#59; commercial paper program&#59; advertising revenue&#59; revenue and revenue growth&#59; membership growth&#59; operating income, operating margin, net income, earnings per share, capital allocation, and free cash flow.
